{ Room } from \"matrix-js-sdk/src/models/room\";\nimport { MatrixEvent } from \"matrix-js-sdk/src/models/event\";\nimport { EventType } from \"matrix-js-sdk/src/@types/event\";\nimport { M_BEACON } from \"matrix-js-sdk/src/@types/beacon\";\n\nimport { MatrixClientPeg } from \"./MatrixClientPeg\";\nimport shouldHideEvent from \"./shouldHideEvent\";\nimport { haveRendererForEvent } from \"./events/EventTileFactory\";\nimport SettingsStore from \"./settings/SettingsStore\";\n\n/**\n * Returns true if this event arriving in a room should affect the room's\n * count of unread messages\n *\n * @param {Object} ev The event\n * @returns {boolean} True if the given event should affect the unread message count\n */\nexport function eventTriggersUnreadCount(ev: MatrixEvent): boolean {\n    if (ev.getSender() === MatrixClientPeg.get().credentials.userId) {\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    switch (ev.getType()) {\n        case EventType.RoomMember:\n        case EventType.RoomThirdPartyInvite:\n        case EventType.CallAnswer:\n        case EventType.CallHangup:\n        case EventType.RoomCanonicalAlias:\n        case EventType.RoomServerAcl:\n        case M_BEACON.name:\n        case M_BEACON.altName:\n            return false;\n    }\n\n    if (ev.isRedacted()) return false;\n    return haveRendererForEvent(ev, false /* hidden messages should never trigger unread counts anyways */);\n}\n\n/**\n * Determines if a timeline (array of events) has unread messages given a\n * read-up-to event ID. Returns true if any relevant event after the receipt\n * was sent by someone other than the current user.\n */\nfunction timelineHasUnread(timeline: MatrixEvent[], readUpToId: string | null, myUserId: string): boolean {\n    // If the last event was sent by me, it's not unread\n    if (timeline.length && timeline[timeline.length - 1].getSender() === myUserId) {\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    for (let i = timeline.length - 1; i >= 0; --i) {\n        const ev = timeline[i];\n\n        if (ev.getId() === readUpToId) {\n            // We've reached the read receipt; nothing more recent counts\n            return false;\n        } else if (!shouldHideEvent(ev) && eventTriggersUnreadCount(ev)) {\n            // Found an unread relevant event before the receipt\n            return true;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Didn't find the receipt; assume unread if there are any relevant events\n    return true;\n}\n\nexport function doesRoomHaveUnreadMessages(room: Room): boolean {\n    if (SettingsStore.getValue(\"feature_sliding_sync\")) {\n        // TODO: https://github.com/vector-im/element-web/issues/23207\n        // Sliding Sync doesn't support unread indicator dots (yet...)\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    const myUserId = MatrixClientPeg.get().getUserId();\n\n    // Check the main room timeline\n    const mainReadUpToId = room.getEventReadUpTo(myUserId);\n    if (timelineHasUnread(room.timeline, mainReadUpToId, myUserId)) {\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    // Check each thread individually\n    if (SettingsStore.getValue(\"feature_thread\")) {\n        for (const thread of room.getThreads()) {\n            const threadTimeline = thread.events;\n            if (!threadTimeline || threadTimeline.length === 0) continue;\n\n            // Get the read receipt for this thread\n            const threadReadUpToId = room.getEventReadUpTo(myUserId, false) ?? \"./events/EventTileFactory\";\nimport SettingsStore from \"./settings/SettingsStore\";\n\n/**\n * Returns true if this event arriving in a room should affect the room's\n * count of unread messages\n *\n * @param {Object} ev The event\n * @returns {boolean} True if the given event should affect the unread message count\n */\nexport function eventTriggersUnreadCount(ev: MatrixEvent): boolean {\n    if (ev.getSender() === MatrixClientPeg.get().credentials.userId) {\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    switch (ev.getType()) {\n        case EventType.RoomMember:\n        case EventType.RoomThirdPartyInvite:\n        case EventType.CallAnswer:\n        case EventType.CallHangup:\n        case EventType.RoomCanonicalAlias:\n        case EventType.RoomServerAcl:\n        case M_BEACON.name:\n        case M_BEACON.altName:\n            return false;\n    }\n\n    if (ev.isRedacted()) return false;\n    return haveRendererForEvent(ev, false /* hidden messages should never trigger unread counts anyways */);\n}\n\n/**\n * Determines if a timeline (array of events) has unread messages given a\n * read-up-to event ID. Returns true if any relevant event after the receipt\n * was sent by someone other than the current user.\n */\nfunction timelineHasUnread(timeline: MatrixEvent[], readUpToId: string | null, myUserId: string): boolean {\n    // If the last event was sent by me, it's not unread\n    if (timeline.length && timeline[timeline.length - 1].getSender() === myUserId) {\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    for (let i = timeline.length - 1; i >= 0; --i) {\n        const ev = timeline[i];\n\n        if (ev.getId() === readUpToId) {\n            // We've reached the read receipt; nothing more recent counts\n            return false;\n        } else if (!shouldHideEvent(ev) && eventTriggersUnreadCount(ev)) {\n            // Found an unread relevant event before the receipt\n            return true;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Didn't find the receipt; assume unread if there are any relevant events\n    return true;\n}\n\nexport function doesRoomHaveUnreadMessages(room: Room): boolean {\n    if (SettingsStore.getValue(\"feature_sliding_sync\")) {\n        // TODO: https://github.com/vector-im/element-web/issues/23207\n        // Sliding Sync doesn't support unread indicator dots (yet...)\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    const myUserId = MatrixClientPeg.get().getUserId();\n\n    // Check the main room timeline\n    const mainReadUpToId = room.getEventReadUpTo(myUserId);\n    if (timelineHasUnread(room.timeline, mainReadUpToId, myUserId)) {\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    // Check each thread individually\n    if (SettingsStore.getValue(\"feature_thread\")) {\n        for (const thread of room.getThreads()) {\n            const threadTimeline = thread.events;\n            if (!threadTimeline || threadTimeline.length === 0) continue;\n\n            // Get the read receipt for this thread\n            const threadReadUpToId = room.getEventReadUpTo(myUserId, false) ?? null;\n\n            // Try to find a thread-specific receipt\n            let threadReceiptId: string | null = null;\n            for (let i = threadTimeline.length - 1; i >= 0; --i) {\n                const ev = threadTimeline[i];\n                const receipt = room.getEventReadUpTo(myUserId);\n                if (ev.getId() === receipt) {\n                    threadReceiptId = receipt;\n                    break;\n                }\n            }\n\n            if (threadHasUnread(threadTimeline, threadReceiptId, myUserId)) {\n                return true;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    return false;\n}\n\nfunction threadHasUnread(timeline: MatrixEvent[], readUpToId: string | null, myUserId: string): boolean {\n    // If the last event was sent by me, it's not unread\n    if (timeline.length && timeline[timeline.length - 1].getSender() === myUserId) {\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    for (let i = timeline.length - 1; i >= 0; --i) {\n        const ev = timeline[i];\n\n        if (ev.getId() === readUpToId) {\n            return false;\n        } else if (!shouldHideEvent(ev) && eventTriggersUnreadCount(ev)) {\n            return true;\n        }\n    }\n\n    return timeline.length > 0;\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

*\n * @param {Object} ev The event\n * @returns {boolean} True if the given event should affect the unread message count\n */\nexport function eventTriggersUnreadCount(ev: MatrixEvent): boolean {\n    if (ev.getSender() === MatrixClientPeg.get().credentials.userId) {\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    switch (ev.getType()) {\n        case EventType.RoomMember:\n        case EventType.RoomThirdPartyInvite:\n        case EventType.CallAnswer:\n        case EventType.CallHangup:\n        case EventType.RoomCanonicalAlias:\n        case EventType.RoomServerAcl:\n        case trigger unread counts anyways */);\n}\n\n/**\n * Determines if a timeline (array of events) has unread messages given a\n * read-up-to event ID. Returns true if any relevant event after the receipt\n * was sent by someone other than the current user.\n */\nfunction timelineHasUnread(timeline: MatrixEvent[], readUpToId: string | null, myUserId: string): boolean {\n    // If the last event was sent by me, it's not unread\n    if (timeline.length && timeline[timeline.length - 1].getSender() === myUserId) {\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    for (let i = timeline.length - 1; i >= 0; --i) {\n        const ev = timeline[i];\n\n        if (ev.getId() === readUpToId) {\n            // We've reached the read receipt; nothing more recent counts\n            return false;\n        } else if (!shouldHideEvent(ev) && eventTriggersUnreadCount(ev)) {\n            // Found an unread relevant event before the receipt\n            return true;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Didn't find the receipt; assume unread if there are any relevant events\n    return true;\n}\n\nexport function doesRoomHaveUnreadMessages(room: Room): boolean {\n    if (SettingsStore.getValue(\"feature_sliding_sync\")) {\n        // TODO: https://github.com/vector-im/element-web/issues/23207\n        // Sliding Sync doesn't support unread indicator dots (yet...)\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    const myUserId = MatrixClientPeg.get().getUserId();\n\n    // Check the main room timeline\n    const mainReadUpToId = room.getEventReadUpTo(myUserId);\n    if (timelineHasUnread(room.timeline, mainReadUpToId, myUserId)) {\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    // Check each thread individually\n    if (SettingsStore.getValue(\"feature_thread\")) {\n        for (const thread of room.getThreads()) {\n            const threadTimeline = thread.events;\n            if (!threadTimeline || threadTimeline.length === 0) continue;\n\n            // Get the read receipt for this thread\n            const threadReadUpToId = room.getEventReadUpTo(myUserId, false) ?? null;\n\n            // Try to find a thread-specific receipt\n            let threadReceiptId: string | null = null;\n            for (let i = threadTimeline.length - 1; i >= 0; --i) {\n                const ev = threadTimeline[i];\n                const receipt = room.getEventReadUpTo(myUserId);\n                if (ev.getId() === receipt) {\n                    threadReceiptId = receipt;\n                    break;\n                }\n            }\n\n            if (threadHasUnread(threadTimeline, threadReceiptId, myUserId)) {\n                return true;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    return false;\n}\n\nfunction threadHasUnread(timeline: MatrixEvent[], readUpToId: string | null, myUserId: string): boolean {\n    // If the last event was sent by me, it's not unread\n    if (timeline.length && timeline[timeline.length - 1].getSender() === myUserId) {\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    for (let i = timeline.length - 1; i >= 0; --i) {\n        const ev = timeline[i];\n\n        if (ev.getId() === readUpToId) {\n            return false;\n        } else if (!shouldHideEvent(ev) && eventTriggersUnreadCount(ev)) {\n            return true;\n        }\n    }\n\n    return timeline.length > 0;\n}\n","numLines":144,"startLine":1,"totalLines":144}}}

function eventTriggersUnreadCount(ev: MatrixEvent): boolean {\n    if (ev.getSender() === MatrixClientPeg.get().credentials.userId) {\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    switch (ev.getType()) {\n        case EventType.RoomMember:\n        case EventType.RoomThirdPartyInvite:\n        case EventType.CallAnswer:\n        case EventType.CallHangup:\n        case EventType.RoomCanonicalAlias:\n        case EventType.RoomServerAcl:\n        case M_BEACON.name:\n        case M_BEACON.altName:\n            return false;\n    }\n\n    if (ev.isRedacted()) return false;\n    return haveRendererForEvent(ev, false /* hidden messages should never trigger unread counts anyways */);\n}\n\n/**\n * Determines if a given timeline has unread messages, given a read-up-to event ID.\n * Ignores events sent by the current user and non-renderable events.\n */\nfunction timelineHasUnreadMessages(timeline: MatrixEvent[], readUpToId: string | null, myUserId: string): boolean {\n    // If the last event was sent by the current user, the timeline is considered read.\n    if (timeline.length && timeline[timeline.length - 1].getSender() === myUserId) {\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    // Loop through events most-recent-first\n    for (let i = timeline.length - 1; i >= 0; --i) {\n        const ev = timeline[i];\n\n        if (ev.getId() === readUpToId) {\n            // We've
